        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





PDFium uses Little-CMS to support ICC profiles. I used AFLSmart fuzzer to fuzz the library and I found a Heap Buffer Overwrite of size 4. I have attached a fuzzed ICC profile that can trigger the bug and following is what ASAN says. It seems to me that there is something wrong in the cmsReadTag function. This bug exists even after all the recent fixes of Little-CMS.



<span class="line"><!---->PDFium uses Little-CMS to support ICC profiles. I used AFLSmart fuzzer to fuzz the library and I found a Heap Buffer Overwrite of size 4. I have attached a fuzzed ICC profile that can trigger the bug and following is what ASAN says. It seems to me that there is something wrong in the cmsReadTag function. This bug exists even after all the recent fixes of Little-CMS.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

Chrome Version: possibly all



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: possibly all<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: possible all



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: possible all<!----></span>



<br>





Little-CMS: up to newest version (Rev 1c3ccf47)



<span class="line"><!---->Little-CMS: up to newest version (Rev 1c3ccf47)<!----></span>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Use the following test driver



<span class="line"><!---->Use the following test driver<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





#include <stdint.h>



<span class="line"><!---->#include &lt;stdint.h&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





#include "lcms2.h"



<span class="line"><!---->#include "lcms2.h"<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





void ReadAllTags(cmsHPROFILE h) {



<span class="line"><!---->void ReadAllTags(cmsHPROFILE h) {<!----></span>



<br>





    cmsInt32Number i, n;



<span class="line"><!---->    cmsInt32Number i, n;<!----></span>



<br>





    cmsTagSignature sig;



<span class="line"><!---->    cmsTagSignature sig;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    n = cmsGetTagCount(h);



<span class="line"><!---->    n = cmsGetTagCount(h);<!----></span>



<br>





    for (i=0; i < n; i++) {



<span class="line"><!---->    for (i=0; i &lt; n; i++) {<!----></span>



<br>





        sig = cmsGetTagSignature(h, i);



<span class="line"><!---->        sig = cmsGetTagSignature(h, i);<!----></span>



<br>





        if (cmsReadTag(h, sig) == NULL) return;



<span class="line"><!---->        if (cmsReadTag(h, sig) == NULL) return;<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





int main(int argc, char* argv[]) {



<span class="line"><!---->int main(int argc, char* argv[]) {<!----></span>



<br>





  cmsHPROFILE h = cmsOpenProfileFromFile(argv[1], "rb");



<span class="line"><!---->  cmsHPROFILE h = cmsOpenProfileFromFile(argv[1], "rb");<!----></span>



<br>





  if (!h) return 0;



<span class="line"><!---->  if (!h) return 0;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  ReadAllTags(h);



<span class="line"><!---->  ReadAllTags(h);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  cmsCloseProfile(h);



<span class="line"><!---->  cmsCloseProfile(h);<!----></span>



<br>





  return 0;



<span class="line"><!---->  return 0;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>

hello, regarding 



<span class="line"><!---->hello, regarding <!----></span>





comment #15



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c15"><!---->comment #15<!----></a>





: we appreciate you reporting this to us; while vulnerabilities in our third-party dependencies are eligible for VRP rewards (g.co/chrome/vrp), they must also impact Chrome to be eligible for a VRP reward. 



<span class="line"><!---->: we appreciate you reporting this to us; while vulnerabilities in our third-party dependencies are eligible for VRP rewards (g.co/chrome/vrp), they must also impact Chrome to be eligible for a VRP reward. <!----></span>



<br>





Since this issue does not impact Chrome, it would not be eligible for a reward. If you any of the issues you've found in Little CMS do impact a configuration of Chrome that ships to users, it will be eligible for a potential reward and would be reviewed by the VRP Panel to determine that. 



<span class="line"><!---->Since this issue does not impact Chrome, it would not be eligible for a reward. If you any of the issues you've found in Little CMS do impact a configuration of Chrome that ships to users, it will be eligible for a potential reward and would be reviewed by the VRP Panel to determine that. <!----></span>



<br>





Thank you!



<span class="line"><!---->Thank you!<!----></span>

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;

          border-collapse: collapse;

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
